// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        #10 t = 1; // Toggle back
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep t low to maintain the state
        
        // Finish the simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Testbench
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs

    end

    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

    output q

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1"
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Toggling back to 0 to hold the state

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        #10 t = 1; // Toggle back
        #10 t = 0; // Maintain state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

endmodule

    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (

        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs
    initial begin
        $monitor("At time %t: clk = %b, reset = %b, t = %b, q = %b", $time, clk, reset, t, q);
    end

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Ensure that T is toggled back

        // Finish simulation
        #30 $finish;
    end

endmodule

        // Initialize inputs

        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to the "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Keep it stable to observe the state

        // Finish the simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

    // Monitor outputs

    output q

    reg reset;

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1"
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Toggling again to maintain the state

        // Finish simulation
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;
        
        // Toggle to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Hold state
        #10 t = 1; // Toggle back
        #10 t = 0; // Hold state
        
        // Finish simulation
        #20 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // 10 time units period
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;

        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle the T flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0;

        // End simulation after some time
        #50 $finish;
    end

endmodule

        #10 t = 0;

// You are given a T flip-flop module with the following declaration:

module tff (
    input clk,
    input reset,   // active-high synchronous reset
    input t,       // toggle
    output q
);

// Write a testbench that instantiates one tff and will reset the T flip-flop then toggle it to the "1" state.

module top_module ();



verilog
    reg clk;
    reg reset;
    reg t;
    wire q;

    // Instantiate the T flip-flop
    tff uut (
        .clk(clk),
        .reset(reset),
        .t(t),
        .q(q)
    );

    // Clock generation
    initial begin
        clk = 0;
        forever #5 clk = ~clk; // Toggle clock every 5 time units
    end

    // Test sequence
    initial begin
        // Initialize inputs
        reset = 0;
        t = 0;
        
        // Apply reset
        #10 reset = 1;
        #10 reset = 0;

        // Toggle T to set the flip-flop to "1" state
        #10 t = 1;
        #10 t = 0; // Ensure that T is toggled back

        // Finish simulation
        #30 $finish;
    end

endmodule
